ror && (
              <Alert variant="destructive" className="border-destructive bg-destructive/10">
                <AlertDescription className="text-destructive text-sm space-y-1">
                  <p>{error}</p>
                  {(error.includes('无效') || error.includes('过期')) && (
                    <p className="text-xs opacity-80">请前往 GitHub → Settings → Developer settings → Personal access tokens 重新生成</p>
                  )}
                  {error.includes('权限') && (
                    <p className="text-xs opacity-80">生成 Token 时请勾选：<code className="bg-destructive/20 px-1 rounded">repo</code> <code className="bg-destructive/20 px-1 rounded">user</code> <code className="bg-destructive/20 px-1 rounded">notifications</code></p>
                  )}
                </AlertDescription>
              </Alert>
            )}

            <Button
              type="submit"
              disabled={loading || !token.trim()}
              className="w-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90 font-medium"
            >
              {loading ? (
                <span className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="w-4 h-4 border-2 border-primary-foreground/30 border-t-primary-foreground rounded-full animate-spin" />
                  验证中...
                </span>
              ) : '令牌登录'}
            </Button>
          </form>
        </div>

        {/* 提示信息 */}
        <div className="mt-4 bg-card border border-border rounded-xl p-4 space-y-3">
          <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">如何获取 Personal Access Token？</h3>
          <ol className="text-xs text-muted-foreground space-y-1 list-decimal list-inside">
            <li>登录 GitHub，进入 Settings → Developer Settings</li>
            <li>选择 Personal access tokens → Tokens (classic)</li>
            <li>点击 Generate new token</li>
            <li>选择所需权限：<code className="bg-secondary px-1 rounded text-foreground">repo</code>、<code className="bg-secondary px-1 rounded text-foreground">notifications</code>、<code className="bg-secondary px-1 rounded text-foreground">user</code></li>
            <li>生成并复制令牌</li>
          </ol>
          <a
            href="https://github.com/settings/tokens/new"
            target="_blank"
            rel="noopener noreferrer"
            className="flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-primary hover:underline"
          >
            <ExternalLink className="w-3 h-3" />
            前往 GitHub 创建令牌
          </a>
        </div>

        {/* 安全说明 */}
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center mt-4 text-pretty">
          令牌与授权凭证仅保存在本地浏览器中，不会上传至任何服务器
        </p>
      </div>

      {/* OAuth Device Flow 对话框 */}
      <OAuthDialog
        open={oauthOpen}
        onOpenChange={setOauthOpen}
        onSuccess={handleOAuthSuccess}
      />
    </div>
  );
}
```

# 推送到 main 分支时自动构建并发布到 gh-pages 分支，同时生成可内嵌 APK 的 dist.zip
name: Deploy to GitHub Pages

New String: ```
# GitHub Pages 自动部署工作流
# 推送到 main 分支时自动构建并发布到 GitHub Pages，同时生成可内嵌 APK 的 dist.zip
name: Deploy to GitHub Pages

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  workflow_dispatch: # 支持手动触发

# 设置 GITHUB_TOKEN 权限以允许部署到 GitHub Pages
permissions:
  contents: read
  pages: write
  id-token: write

# 只允许一个并发部署，新部署会取消正在进行的部署
concurrency:
  group: pages
  cancel-in-progress: true

jobs:
  build-and-deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: 检出代码
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: 安装 pnpm
        uses: pnpm/action-setup@v4
        with:
          version: 9
          # pnpm/action-setup 自身会缓存 store；
          # 不在 setup-node 中再配 cache: pnpm，
          # 避免 lockfile 不存在时报 "Dependencies lock file is not found"

      - name: 设置 Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          # cache: pnpm  ← 已移除；lockfile 首次提交前不存在会导致此步骤失败

      - name: 安装依赖
        # --frozen-lockfile 确保 CI 使用锁定版本，不意外升级依赖
        run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: 构建
        # package.json 的 build 脚本仅用于本地 lint，
        # CI 中直接调用 vite build 避免被 echo 跳过
        run: pnpm exec vite build

      # ── APK 内嵌产物 ──────────────────────────────────────────
      # 将 dist/ 压缩为 dist.zip，可直接复制到 Android assets/ 目录
      # 在 WebView 中通过 file:///android_asset/index.html 加载
      - name: 打包 WebView APK 可用 dist.zip
        run: cd dist && zip -r ../dist.zip . && cd ..

      - name: 上传 dist.zip 为 Actions Artifact
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: webview-apk-dist
          path: dist.zip
          retention-days: 30
      # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

      - name: 配置 GitHub Pages
        uses: actions/configure-pages@v5

      - name: 上传构建产物
        uses: actions/upload-pages-artifact@v3
        with:
          path: dist

      - name: 部署到 GitHub Pages
        id: deployment
        uses: actions/deploy-pages@v4

```

Create an Android project with WebView that loads `file:///android_asset/index.html`\n3. Copy the `dist/` contents into `app/src/main/assets/`\n4. Build the Android project with Gradle to get the APK\n\nThis requires:\n- Setting up JDK 17+ in GitHub Actions\n- Setting up Android SDK (via `android-actions/setup-android` or manual setup)\n- Having an Android project in the repo\n\nThe challenge is: we need an Android project. JDK 17\n2. Android SDK with build-tools\n3. Gradle\n\nThe `android-actions/setup-android@v3` action handles this automatically on ubuntu-latest (which already has Android SDK pre-installed on GitHub\'s ubuntu-latest runners!).\n\nYes, `ubuntu-latest` on GitHub Actions already has Android SDK installed at `/usr/local/lib/android/sdk`. So we don\'t need a separate setup action for the SDK.\n\nBut we do need to set `ANDROID_HOME` or `ANDROID_SDK_ROOT` and install specific build-tools if needed.\n\nLet me simplify - just use JDK + the pre-installed Android SDK on ubuntu-latest:\n\n```yaml\n- name: Setup JDK 17\n  uses: actions/setup-java@v4\n  with:\n    java-version: \'17\'\n    distribution: \'temurin\'\n\n- name: Setup Gradle\n  uses: gradle/actions/setup-gradle@v3\n  with:\n    gradle-version: \'8.11\'\n\n- name: Copy web assets\n  run: mkdir -p android/app/src/main/assets && cp -r dist/. android/app/src/main/assets/\n\n- name: Build debug APK\n  working-directory: android\n  env:\n    ANDROID_HOME: /usr/local/lib/android/sdk\n  run: gradle assembleDebug\n```\n\nNow for the Android project itself. android.os.Bundle\nimport android.webkit.WebResourceRequest\nimport android.webkit.WebSettings\nimport android.webkit.WebView\nimport android.webkit.WebViewClient\nimport androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity\n\nclass MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {\n\n    private lateinit var webView: WebView\n\n    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")\n    override fun   request: WebResourceRequest?\n            ): Boolean {\n                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false\n                // 内部 file:// 链接由 WebView 自己处理\n                if (url.startsWith("file://")) return false\n                // HTTPS 链接（GitHub API 等）也由 WebView 处理\n                if (url.startsWith("https://") || url.startsWith("http://")) return false\n                return true\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (savedInstanceState != null) {\n            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)\n        } else {\n            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")\n        }\n    }\n\n    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {\n        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)\n        webView.saveState(outState)\n    }\n\n    override fun onBackPressed() {\n        if (webView.canGoBack()) {\n            webView.goBack()\n        } else {\n            super.onBackPressed()\n name: 下载 Web 构建产物\n        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4\n        with:\n          name: web-dist\n          path: dist\n      \n      - name: 复制 Web 资源到 Android assets\n        run: |\n          mkdir -p android/app/src/main/assets\n          cp -r dist/. android/app/src/main/assets/\n      \n      - name: 设置 JDK 17\n        uses: actions/setup-java@v4\n        with:\n          java-version: \'17\'\n          distribution: \'temurin\'\n      \n      - name: 设置 Gradle\n        uses: gradle/actions/setup-gradle@v3\n        with:\n          gradle-version: \'8.7\'\n      \n      - name: 生成 local.properties\n        run: echo "sdk.dir=$ANDROID_HOME" > android/local.properties\n      \n      - name: 接受 Android SDK 许可证\n        run: yes | $ANDROID_HOME/cmdline-tools/latest/bin/sdkmanager --licenses || true\n      \n      - name: 构建 Debug APK\n        working-directory: android\n        run: gradle assembleDebug\n      \n      - name: 上传 APK 产物\n        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4\n        with:\n          name: github-manager-apk\n          path: android/app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk\n          retention-days: 30\n```\n\nThis is clean and organized. Let me now write all the Android project files.\n\nOne concern: `gradle/actions/setup-gradle@v3` - will it find the android project without a wrapper? Thought: 
Command: create
Created File with Text:
```
package com.github.manager

import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.View
import android.view.WindowManager
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity
import androidx.core.view.WindowCompat
import androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsControllerCompat

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        // 全屏沉浸式——让 WebView 延伸到状态栏 / 导航栏下方
        WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)
        window.statusBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        WindowInsetsControllerCompat(window, window.decorView).apply {
            isAppearanceLightStatusBars = false
            isAppearanceLightNavigationBars = false
        }

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)

        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true          // localStorage / sessionStorage
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true            // 读取 assets 内的 index.html
            allowContentAccess = true
            // 允许 file:// 页面访问 https:// (GitHub API)
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            // 视口自适应
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            // 禁用内置缩放控件，由 Web 端 viewport meta 控制
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            // 媒体自动播放
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }

        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.TRANSPARENT)

        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                // file:// 和 https:// 均在 WebView 内处理（GitHub API + OAuth Device Flow）
                if (url.startsWith("file://") ||
                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
                    url.startsWith("http://")
                ) return false
                return true
            }

            override fun onPageFinished(view: WebView?, url: String?) {
                super.onPageFinished(view, url)
                // 页面加载完成后隐藏背景防止白屏闪烁
                webView.visibility = View.VISIBLE
            }
        }

        // 屏幕旋转等配置变化时恢复页面状态，避免重新加载
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.visibility = View.INVISIBLE // 加载前隐藏，onPageFinished 后显示
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
            webView.goBack()
        } else {
            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }
}

```

</action>

# GitHub Pages 自动部署工作流
# 推送到 main 分支时自动构建并发布到 GitHub Pages，同时生成可内嵌 APK 的 dist.zip
name: Deploy to GitHub Pages

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  workflow_dispatch: # 支持手动触发

# 设置 GITHUB_TOKEN 权限以允许部署到 GitHub Pages
permissions:
  contents: read
  pages: write
  id-token: write

# 只允许一个并发部署，新部署会取消正在进行的部署

  group: pages
  cancel-in-progress: true

jobs:
  build-and-deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: 检出代码
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: 安装 pnpm
        uses: pnpm/action-setup@v4
        with:
          version: 9
          # pnpm/action-setup 自身会缓存 store；
          # 不在 setup-node 中再配 cache: pnpm，
          # 避免 lockfile 不存在时报 "Dependencies lock file is not found"

        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          # cache: pnpm  ← 已移除；lockfile 首次提交前不存在会导致此步骤失败

      - name: 安装依赖
        # --frozen-lockfile 确保 CI 使用锁定版本，不意外升级依赖

      - name: 构建
        # package.json 的 build 脚本仅用于本地 lint，
        # CI 中直接调用 vite build 避免被 echo 跳过
        run: pnpm exec vite build

      # ── APK 内嵌产物 ──────────────────────────────────────────

      # 在 WebView 中通过 file:///android_asset/index.html 加载

      # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

New String: ```
# GitHub Pages 自动部署 + Android APK 构建工作流
# 推送到 main 分支时：
#   1. 构建 Web 应用（dist/）
#   2. 部署到 GitHub Pages
#   3. 打包 Android APK（WebView 壳 + dist/ 资源）
name: Deploy & Build APK

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  workflow_dispatch: # 支持手动触发

# GITHUB_TOKEN 权限：Pages 部署需要 pages + id-token
permissions:
  contents: read
  pages: write
  id-token: write

# 同组并发：新部署取消旧部署（仅影响 Pages，APK 构建不受影响）
concurrency:
  group: pages
  cancel-in-progress: true

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
jobs:

  # ── Job 1：构建 Web 应用 ───────────────────────────────────────
  build-web:
    name: 构建 Web 应用
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: 检出代码
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: 安装 pnpm
        uses: pnpm/action-setup@v4
        with:
          version: 9
          # pnpm/action-setup 自身处理 store 缓存；
          # 不在 setup-node 中配 cache: pnpm，
          # 避免首次提交时 lockfile 不存在导致步骤失败

      - name: 设置 Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20

      - name: 安装依赖
        run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: 构建 Web 应用
        run: pnpm exec vite build

      - name: 上传 Web 构建产物（供后续 Job 使用）
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: web-dist
          path: dist
          retention-days: 1   # 仅在本次 workflow 期间保留

      - name: 配置 GitHub Pages
        uses: actions/configure-pages@v5

      - name: 上传 Pages 产物
        uses: actions/upload-pages-artifact@v3
        with:
          path: dist

  # ── Job 2：部署到 GitHub Pages ─────────────────────────────────
  deploy-pages:
    name: 部署到 GitHub Pages
    needs: build-web
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment:
      name: github-pages
      url: ${{ steps.deployment.outputs.page_url }}
    steps:
      - name: 部署到 GitHub Pages
        id: deployment
        uses: actions/deploy-pages@v4

  # ── Job 3：构建 Android APK ────────────────────────────────────
  build-apk:
    name: 构建 Android APK
    needs: build-web
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: 检出代码（含 android/ 项目源码）
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: 下载 Web 构建产物
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: web-dist
          path: dist

      - name: 将 Web 资源复制到 Android assets
        run: |
          mkdir -p android/app/src/main/assets
          cp -r dist/. android/app/src/main/assets/

      - name: 设置 JDK 17
        uses: actions/setup-java@v4
        with:
          java-version: '17'
          distribution: 'temurin'

      - name: 设置 Gradle 8.7
        uses: gradle/actions/setup-gradle@v3
        with:
          gradle-version: '8.7'
          # 缓存 Gradle 依赖，加快后续构建
          cache-read-only: false

      - name: 生成 local.properties（指向预装 Android SDK）
        run: echo "sdk.dir=$ANDROID_HOME" > android/local.properties

      - name: 接受 Android SDK 许可证
        run: |
          yes | $ANDROID_HOME/cmdline-tools/latest/bin/sdkmanager --licenses 2>/dev/null || true

      - name: 构建 Debug APK
        working-directory: android
        run: gradle assembleDebug --no-daemon

      - name: 上传 APK 产物
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: github-manager-apk
          path: android/app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk
          retention-days: 30

```

<action>
AgentThinkAction(thought='\nThe user is experiencing a black screen when loading the APK on Android. Let me think about what could cause this.\n\nThe app is a React/Vite web app packaged in a WebView. When built with `vite build`, assets are placed in `dist/`. The APK loads from `file:///android_asset/index.html`.\n\nCommon causes of black screen with WebView + file:// assets:\n\n1. **Vite build base path issue**: By default, Vite builds with `base: \'/\'` which generates absolute paths like `/assets/index-xxx.js`. When loaded from `file:///android_asset/index.html`, the browser tries to resolve `/assets/...` as `file:///assets/...` (root of filesystem), not `file:///android_asset/assets/...`. This is the MOST LIKELY cause.\n\n   Fix: Set `base: \'./\'` in `vite.config.ts` to use relative paths.\n\n2. **React Router with BrowserRouter**: BrowserRouter uses the History API which doesn\'t work with `file://` URLs. Need to use `HashRouter` instead.\n\n3. **CORS issues**: file:// protocol has strict CORS policies. \n\n4. **Missing files**: The assets might not be copied correctly.\n\nThe #1 issue is almost certainly the **Vite base path**. With `base: \'/\'`, the built `index.html` will have:\n```html\n<script type="module" src="/assets/index-xxx.js"></script>\n```\n\nBut with `file://` protocol, `/assets/` resolves to the filesystem root, not the assets folder. Setting `base: \'./\'` generates:\n```html\n<script type="module" src="./assets/index-xxx.js"></script>\n```\n\nWhich correctly resolves relative to `index.html`.\n\nThe #2 issue is **React Router BrowserRouter vs HashRouter**. The app likely uses BrowserRouter. With `file://`, BrowserRouter doesn\'t work properly because there\'s no server to handle URL paths. Or the whole `<item>` might be skipped.\n\nActually wait - looking at the XML more carefully:\n```xml\n<item name="android:windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode" tools:ignore="NewApi">shortEdges</item>\n```\n\nHere `tools:ignore` is an attribute on the `<item>` element. The element\'s `name` attribute is `android:windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode` and its text content is `shortEdges`. The `tools:ignore="NewApi"` is an attribute that AAPT2/aapt typically processes. Without `xmlns:tools`, AAPT2 might:\n- Ignore the undeclared namespace attribute (likely behavior)\n- Fail with a parse error\n\nIf AAPT2 ignores the unknown namespace attribute, the item would still be processed correctly (name = windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode, value = shortEdges). This might be fine on API 28+.\n\nActually, `android:windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode` was added in API 28. On minSdk = 26 devices, this attribute would be unknown and Android would ignore it. So it\'s safe to use. The `tools:ignore` was just to suppress a lint warning.\n\nSo the themes.xml might actually be fine (AAPT2 just processes the item, ignoring the undeclared tools: attribute). But it\'s still a bad practice.\n\n2. **`webView.visibility = View.INVISIBLE`**: This is a significant issue. Let me trace the flow:\n   - Activity starts → WebView is INVISIBLE\n   - `loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")` is called\n   - `onPageFinished` fires → WebView becomes VISIBLE\n   \n   The issue: for a React + Vite app with code splitting, `onPageFinished` fires when the main HTML document is loaded. But the React app might not have rendered by then. However, the WebView would show the HTML background (which is initially `#0d1117` since we set it in themes.xml). After `onPageFinished`, visibility is set to VISIBLE, and the user sees... the dark background while JS loads.\n   \n   But if there\'s a JS error and React never renders, the user sees the dark background indefinitely = "black screen".\n\n3. **`manualChunks` + `file://` dynamic imports**: This is the most likely root cause. The Vite config has `manualChunks` splitting code into vendor-react, vendor-router, vendor-radix, vendor-charts, vendor-markdown, vendor-misc chunks. These are loaded as dynamic imports.\n   \n   In Android WebView with `file://` URLs:\n   - Static `<script type="module" src="./assets/main.js">` works fine\n   - Dynamic `import(\'./assets/vendor-react.js\')` from within a module file might be restricted\n   \n   Starting from Chrome 90+ (WebView equivalent), cross-origin file:// access is blocked, but SAME directory file:// access should still work. However, there\'s been inconsistency across Android versions.\n\n4. **Module preload**: The `<link rel="modulepreload" href="./assets/vendor-react.js">` tags might cause WebView to pre-fetch files, and if there\'s a restriction on file:// access, this could fail silently.\n\n**The definitive fix:**\n\n1. **Disable code splitting / manual chunks** for the WebView build: Single bundle, no dynamic imports\n2. **Remove `modulePreload`**\n3. **Fix themes.xml** to remove undeclared `tools:ignore`\n4. **Fix `webView.visibility`** - just show it directly, no invisible trick\n5. **Add `allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true`** as a safety measure (even though deprecated)\n\nFor disabling code splitting in Vite, I can set:\n```js\nbuild: {\n  rollupOptions: {\n    output: {\n      manualChunks: undefined,  // disable manual chunks\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\nBut this won\'t prevent automatic code splitting from dynamic imports in the source code. To truly create a single bundle:\n```js\nbuild: {\n  rollupOptions: {\n    output: {\n      manualChunks: undefined,\n      inlineDynamicImports: true,  // inline all dynamic imports\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\nWait, but `routes.tsx` uses static imports (not lazy), so there are no dynamic imports in the route definitions. The only dynamic imports might be in library code... Actually, Vite itself might introduce dynamic imports for module federation or similar.\n\nLooking at `routes.tsx`, all pages are statically imported. So the only dynamic imports are the `manualChunks` I introduced. If I remove `manualChunks`, Rollup will try to split chunks based on the module graph, but without explicit lazy routes, it might still create a single bundle (or minimal chunks).\n\nActually with Vite and no `manualChunks` and no `import()` in user code, Rollup should create a single bundle (or very few chunks). Let me simplify:\n\n```js\nbuild: {\n  modulePreload: false,  // disable <link rel="modulepreload"> tags\n  rollupOptions: {\n    output: {\n      manualChunks: undefined,  // let Rollup decide (likely single bundle)\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\nBut wait, there\'s another consideration: the app might use Recharts/React-markdown which are large libraries. A single bundle could be 3-5MB which is large for an APK but acceptable.\n\nActually, looking at this more carefully - the routes are all statically imported. So Vite/Rollup will create:\n- One "entry" chunk (main)\n- Potentially some "shared" chunks if multiple entry points share code\n\nWith a single entry point (main.tsx) and no dynamic imports in user code, Rollup should create a single bundle unless `manualChunks` tells it to split. If I remove `manualChunks`, it should be a single or minimal bundle.\n\nLet me check: does Vite 5 do automatic code splitting even without manualChunks and without dynamic imports? I believe it does for vendor chunks in some configurations, but without explicit dynamic imports, it should not.\n\nOK let me just make the fix simple and definitive:\n\n1. Set `modulePreload: false` in build config\n2. Remove `manualChunks` \n3. Fix MainActivity.kt to remove the visibility trick and add `allowFileAccessFromFileURLs`\n4. Fix themes.xml\n\nActually, I just realized another potential issue. The `themes.xml` has:\n```xml\n<item name="android:windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode" tools:ignore="NewApi">shortEdges</item>\n```\n\nOn Android 8.0 (minSdk=26), this attribute doesn\'t exist (it was added in API 28). If AAPT2 fails to parse this because of the `tools:ignore` syntax issue... Actually wait.\n\nIn AAPT2, when you use an attribute with `tools:ignore`, you need to declare `xmlns:tools="http://schemas.android.com/tools"` at the root element. If not declared, AAPT2 will fail with: "Error: \': attribute not found.\'" or similar.\n\nBut actually, AAPT2 processes tools attributes differently than regular XML parsers. It might:\n1. Fail entirely - no APK built\n2. Ignore the undeclared namespace and process the item normally\n\nIf option 1, the user can\'t install the APK. But they did install it. So either:\n- AAPT2 is lenient (option 2)\n- Or somehow the build succeeded\n\nI\'ll just fix themes.xml to remove the `tools:ignore` since it\'s not needed (the attribute is valid on minSdk 26 devices, Android just ignores unknown attributes gracefully).\n\n**Summary of fixes:**\n1. `vite.config.ts`: Set `modulePreload: false`, remove `manualChunks`\n2. `MainActivity.kt`: Remove visibility trick, add `allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true`\n3. `themes.xml`: Remove `tools:ignore` attribute (undeclared namespace)\n\nLet me code these up now.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

  build: {
    // 关闭 sourcemap，减小 APK 内嵌包体积
    sourcemap: false,
    // 静态资源统一放 assets/ 目录
    assetsDir: "assets",
    chunkSizeWarningLimit: 2000,
    // 关闭 <link rel="modulepreload">：
    // WebView 以 file:// 加载时，modulepreload 会触发额外的文件请求，
    // 在部分 Android 版本中会因 file:// 跨资源限制而静默失败，导致白屏/黑屏
    modulePreload: false,
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        // 不做 manualChunks 拆分：
        // file:// 协议下，动态 import() 跨 chunk 文件在部分 WebView 版本中
        // 受同源策略限制，可能被阻断，导致 React 无法完成初始化渲染。
        // 不拆包后，所有代码合并进少量静态 chunk，WebView 可以顺序加载，无动态 import 权限问题。
        manualChunks: undefined,
      },

                // file:// 和 https:// 均在 WebView 内处理（GitHub API + OAuth Device Flow）

                // 页面加载完成后隐藏背景防止白屏闪烁
                webView.visibility = View.VISIBLE
            }

        // 屏幕旋转等配置变化时恢复页面状态，避免重新加载
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.visibility = View.INVISIBLE // 加载前隐藏，onPageFinished 后显示
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")

        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true

React renders initially with `loading = true` → shows spinner\n5. Auth check completes → redirects to login page\n6. Only reveal content after React is ready.\n2. **React side**: Use `useEffect` in a wrapper component or in `App` to call the Android bridge when ready.\n\nFor the React `useEffect`, I should add it to `App.tsx`. The `notifyReady()` would never be called!\n\nI need to call `notifyReady()` at the App level. Let me restructure:\n\nOption 1: Call it in `App.tsx` in a `useEffect` but with a delay to let auth resolve:\n```tsx\nuseEffect(() => {\n  const timer = setTimeout(() => {\n    (window as any).AndroidBridge?.notifyReady();\n  }, 100);\n  return () => clearTimeout(timer);\n}, []);\n```\n\nBut 100ms might not be enough for auth check.\n\nOption 2: Create an `AppContent` wrapper that uses `useAuth` and calls `notifyReady` when `!loading`:\n```tsx\nfunction AppContent() {\n  const { loading } = useAuth();\n  \n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (!loading) {\n      (window as any).AndroidBridge?.notifyReady();\n    }\n  }, [loading]);\n  \n  return (\n    <Routes>\n      {/* ... */}\n    </Routes>\n  );\n}\n\nconst App = () => (\n  <ErrorBoundary>\n    <Router>\n      <AuthProvider>\n        <AppContent />\n        <Toaster ... />\n      </AuthProvider>\n    </Router>\n  </ErrorBoundary>\n);\n```\n\nThis is cleaner! `AppContent` is inside `AuthProvider` so it has access to `useAuth`, and it notifies Android when auth loading is done (which means the UI is settled - either showing login or the app).\n\nThis is the best approach. Let me implement this.\n\nNow let me write all the changes needed:\n\n1. `src/App.tsx` - Add `AppContent` component with `useEffect`\n2. `android/app/src/main/res/layout/activity_main.xml` - Add splash overlay\n3. `android/app/src/main/java/com/github/manager/MainActivity.kt` - Add JS bridge + splash logic\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

import React from 'react';
import { HashRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { Toaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
import { AuthProvider, useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import MainLayout from '@/components/layouts/MainLayout';
import { ErrorBoundary } from '@/components/common/ErrorBoundary';
import { routes } from './routes';

// 路由守卫：未登录跳转到 /login
function RouteGuard({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const { isAuthenticated, loading } = useAuth();
  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-background">
        <div className="w-8 h-8 border-2 border-primary/30 border-t-primary rounded-full animate-spin" />
      </div>
    );
  }
  if (!isAuthenticated) {
    return <Navigate to="/login" replace />;
  }
  return <>{children}</>;
}

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <Router>
        <AuthProvider>
          <Routes>
            {/* 公开路由（登录页） */}
            {routes
              .filter((r) => r.public)
              .map((route) => (
                <Route key={route.path} path={route.path} element={route.element} />
              ))}

            {/* 受保护路由（需要登录） */}
            {routes
              .filter((r) => !r.public)
              .map((route) => (
                <Route
                  key={route.path}
                  path={route.path}
                  element={
                    <RouteGuard>
                      <MainLayout>{route.element}</MainLayout>
                    </RouteGuard>
                  }
                />
              ))}

            {/* 404 重定向 */}
            <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
          </Routes>
          <Toaster richColors position="top-right" />
        </AuthProvider>
      </Router>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
};

export default App;

New String: ```
import React, { useEffect } from 'react';
import { HashRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { Toaster } from '@/components/ui/sonner';
import { AuthProvider, useAuth } from '@/contexts/AuthContext';
import MainLayout from '@/components/layouts/MainLayout';
import { ErrorBoundary } from '@/components/common/ErrorBoundary';
import { routes } from './routes';

// 路由守卫：未登录跳转到 /login
function RouteGuard({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const { isAuthenticated, loading } = useAuth();
  if (loading) {
    return (
      <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen bg-background">
        <div className="w-8 h-8 border-2 border-primary/30 border-t-primary rounded-full animate-spin" />
      </div>
    );
  }
  if (!isAuthenticated) {
    return <Navigate to="/login" replace />;
  }
  return <>{children}</>;
}

/**
 * 内层路由容器，位于 AuthProvider 内部，可访问 useAuth。
 * 当 auth 加载完成（无论已登录或未登录）后，通知 Android 原生层
 * 隐藏启动遮罩，避免 WebView 初始化过程中的闪烁。
 */
function AppContent() {
  const { loading } = useAuth();

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!loading) {
      // 通知 Android WebView 首屏已就绪，可以隐藏启动遮罩
      // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
      (window as any).AndroidBridge?.notifyReady();
    }
  }, [loading]);

  return (
    <>
      <Routes>
        {/* 公开路由（登录页） */}
        {routes
          .filter((r) => r.public)
          .map((route) => (
            <Route key={route.path} path={route.path} element={route.element} />
          ))}

        {/* 受保护路由（需要登录） */}
        {routes
          .filter((r) => !r.public)
          .map((route) => (
            <Route
              key={route.path}
              path={route.path}
              element={
                <RouteGuard>
                  <MainLayout>{route.element}</MainLayout>
                </RouteGuard>
              }
            />
          ))}

        {/* 404 重定向 */}
        <Route path="*" element={<Navigate to="/" replace />} />
      </Routes>
      <Toaster richColors position="top-right" />
    </>
  );
}

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <Router>
        <AuthProvider>
          <AppContent />
        </AuthProvider>
      </Router>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  );
};

export default App;
```

package com.github.manager

import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity
import androidx.core.view.WindowCompat
import androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsControllerCompat

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        // 全屏沉浸式——让 WebView 延伸到状态栏 / 导航栏下方
        WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)
        window.statusBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        WindowInsetsControllerCompat(window, window.decorView).apply {
            isAppearanceLightStatusBars = false
            isAppearanceLightNavigationBars = false
        }

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)

        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true           // localStorage / sessionStorage（token 存储）
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true             // 允许读取 assets 内的文件
            allowContentAccess = true
            // 允许 file:// 脚本访问同目录其他 file:// 资源（兼容旧版 WebView）
            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
            // 允许 file:// 页面向 https:// 发起网络请求（GitHub API / OAuth）
            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            // 视口自适应，防止页面内容被缩放或裁切
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            // 禁用内置缩放控件，由 Web 端 viewport meta 控制
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }

        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.TRANSPARENT)

        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                // file:// / https:// / http:// 均在 WebView 内处理
                if (url.startsWith("file://") ||
                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
                    url.startsWith("http://")
                ) return false
                return true
            }
        }

        // 屏幕旋转等配置变化时恢复页面状态，避免重新加载
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            // 直接加载，不使用 INVISIBLE→VISIBLE 技巧：
            // onPageFinished 在 React JS 完全渲染前就可能触发，
            // 若之前隐藏 WebView 则 React 不会开始渲染，导致永久黑屏。
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
            webView.goBack()
        } else {
            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }
}

New String: ```
package com.github.manager

import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.os.Handler
import android.os.Looper
import android.view.View
import android.webkit.JavascriptInterface
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity
import androidx.core.view.WindowCompat
import androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsControllerCompat

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView
    private lateinit var splashOverlay: View

    // 防止 notifyReady 被重复调用时多次触发动画
    private var splashDismissed = false

    /**
     * JavaScript 桥接口：React 首屏渲染完成后调用 notifyReady()，
     * 通知 Android 隐藏启动遮罩。
     */
    inner class WebAppBridge {
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyReady() {
            runOnUiThread { dismissSplash() }
        }
    }

    /** 淡出并移除启动遮罩，保证只执行一次。 */
    private fun dismissSplash() {
        if (splashDismissed) return
        splashDismissed = true
        splashOverlay
            .animate()
            .alpha(0f)
            .setDuration(250)
            .withEndAction { splashOverlay.visibility = View.GONE }
            .start()
    }

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        // 全屏沉浸式：延伸到状态栏 / 导航栏下方
        WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)
        window.statusBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        WindowInsetsControllerCompat(window, window.decorView).apply {
            isAppearanceLightStatusBars = false
            isAppearanceLightNavigationBars = false
        }

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)
        splashOverlay = findViewById(R.id.splashOverlay)

        // ── WebView 设置 ──────────────────────────────────────────
        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true           // localStorage / sessionStorage（token 存储）
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true             // 允许读取 assets 内的文件
            allowContentAccess = true
            // 允许 file:// 脚本访问同目录其他 file:// 资源（兼容旧版 WebView）
            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
            // 允许 file:// 页面向 https:// 发起网络请求（GitHub API / OAuth）
            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }

        // WebView 背景与启动遮罩同色，避免遮罩淡出时出现颜色差异
        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor("#0d1117"))

        // ── JavaScript 桥接口 ─────────────────────────────────────
        // React 侧通过 window.AndroidBridge.notifyReady() 触发遮罩消失
        webView.addJavascriptInterface(WebAppBridge(), "AndroidBridge")

        // ── WebViewClient ─────────────────────────────────────────
        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                if (url.startsWith("file://") ||
                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
                    url.startsWith("http://")
                ) return false
                return true
            }
        }

        // ── 超时兜底：5 秒后强制消除遮罩 ────────────────────────────
        // 防止 notifyReady 因异常未被调用时遮罩永远停留
        Handler(Looper.getMainLooper()).postDelayed({ dismissSplash() }, 5000)

        // ── 加载页面 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
            webView.goBack()
        } else {
            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }
}

    43	            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    44	            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
    45	            // 允许 file:// 页面向 https:// 发起网络请求（GitHub API / OAuth）

    47	            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW

    69	                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
    70	                    url.startsWith("http://")
    71	                ) return false
    72	                return true
    73	            }
    74	        }

    77	        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
    78	            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
    79	        } else {
    80	            // 直接加载，不使用 INVISIBLE→VISIBLE 技巧：

    83	            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
    84	        }
    85	    }

cat > /workspace/app-bgc5z86utjwh/android/app/src/main/java/com/github/manager/MainActivity.kt << 'KOTLIN_EOF'
package com.github.manager

import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.os.Handler
import android.os.Looper
import android.view.View
import android.webkit.JavascriptInterface
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity
import androidx.core.view.WindowCompat
import androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsControllerCompat

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView
    private lateinit var splashOverlay: View

    // 防止 notifyReady 被重复调用时多次触发动画
    private var splashDismissed = false

    /**
     * JavaScript 桥接口：React 首屏渲染完成后调用 notifyReady()，
     * 通知 Android 隐藏启动遮罩。
     */
    inner class WebAppBridge {
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyReady() {
            runOnUiThread { dismissSplash() }
        }
    }

    /** 淡出并移除启动遮罩，保证只执行一次。 */
    private fun dismissSplash() {
        if (splashDismissed) return
        splashDismissed = true
        splashOverlay
            .animate()
            .alpha(0f)
            .setDuration(250)
            .withEndAction { splashOverlay.visibility = View.GONE }
            .start()
    }

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        // 全屏沉浸式：延伸到状态栏 / 导航栏下方
        WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)
        window.statusBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        WindowInsetsControllerCompat(window, window.decorView).apply {
            isAppearanceLightStatusBars = false
            isAppearanceLightNavigationBars = false
        }

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)
        splashOverlay = findViewById(R.id.splashOverlay)

        // ── WebView 设置 ──────────────────────────────────────────
        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true           // localStorage / sessionStorage（token 存储）
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true             // 允许读取 assets 内的文件
            allowContentAccess = true
            // 允许 file:// 脚本访问同目录其他 file:// 资源（兼容旧版 WebView）
            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
            // 允许 file:// 页面向 https:// 发起网络请求（GitHub API / OAuth）
            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }

        // WebView 背景与启动遮罩同色，避免遮罩淡出时出现颜色差异
        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor("#0d1117"))

        // ── JavaScript 桥接口 ─────────────────────────────────────
        // React 侧通过 window.AndroidBridge.notifyReady() 触发遮罩消失
        webView.addJavascriptInterface(WebAppBridge(), "AndroidBridge")

        // ── WebViewClient ─────────────────────────────────────────
        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                if (url.startsWith("file://") ||
                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
                    url.startsWith("http://")
                ) return false
                return true
            }
        }

        // ── 超时兜底：5 秒后强制消除遮罩 ────────────────────────────
        // 防止 notifyReady 因异常未被调用时遮罩永远停留
        Handler(Looper.getMainLooper()).postDelayed({ dismissSplash() }, 5000)

        // ── 加载页面 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
            webView.goBack()
        } else {
            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }
}

AgentThinkAction(thought='\nThe user is experiencing a layout overlap with the Android status bar. This is a common issue with WebView apps that use edge-to-edge mode.\n\nThe current setup in MainActivity.kt:\n```kotlin\nWindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)\nwindow.statusBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT\nwindow.navigationBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT\n```\n\nThis enables edge-to-edge mode, which makes the content extend under the status bar and navigation bar. However, the web content doesn\'t add the proper padding to avoid the status bar area.\n\nThe issue is:\n1. `WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)` makes the window extend under system bars\n2. The web content starts from the very top (0,0) which is under the status bar\n3. UI elements at the top of the web page are hidden/unclickable because they\'re behind the status bar\n\nSolutions:\n\n**Option 1: Re-enable system bar fitting**\nThe simplest fix: remove `WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)` and let Android handle the padding naturally. The status bar will push content down.\n\n```kotlin\n// Remove this: WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)\n// Just set opaque status bar colors\nwindow.statusBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")\n```\n\nBut this loses the immersive/edge-to-edge look.\n\n**Option 2: Inject CSS with safe area insets via JavaScript**\nKeep edge-to-edge but inject the status bar height as CSS variable into the web page:\n\n```kotlin\nwebView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {\n    override fun onPageFinished(view: WebView?, url: String?) {\n        super.onPageFinished(view, url)\n        // Inject status bar height as CSS variable\n        val statusBarHeight = getStatusBarHeight()\n        view?.evaluateJavascript(\n            "document.documentElement.style.setProperty(\'--android-status-bar-height\', \'${statusBarHeight}px\');",\n            null\n        )\n    }\n}\n```\n\nThen use `env(safe-area-inset-top)` in CSS or the injected variable.\n\n**Option 3: Use ViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener**\nHandle window insets natively and apply padding to the WebView:\n\n```kotlin\nViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener(webView) { view, insets ->\n    val systemBars = insets.getInsets(WindowInsetsCompat.Type.systemBars())\n    view.setPadding(systemBars.left, systemBars.top, systemBars.right, systemBars.bottom)\n    insets\n}\n```\n\nBut applying padding to WebView might cause visual artifacts.\n\n**Option 4: Disable edge-to-edge (simplest and most reliable)**\nThe most reliable fix for a WebView app is to NOT use edge-to-edge mode. The web content itself can\'t easily handle system bar insets without special meta tags.\n\nRemove `WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)` and set status bar to the same color as the app background:\n\n```kotlin\n// Don\'t set decor to not fit system windows - let Android handle padding\nwindow.statusBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")  // Match app background\nwindow.navigationBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117") // Match app background\n```\n\nThis way the content properly starts BELOW the status bar.\n\n**The best approach for this case:**\n\nFor a WebView app where the web content doesn\'t have native knowledge of system bars, the cleanest fix is **Option 3**: apply window insets as padding to the WebView container. This keeps the edge-to-edge aesthetic while properly pushing content below the status bar.\n\nOR even simpler: **Option 4** - just remove edge-to-edge mode. For a WebView app, edge-to-edge is more trouble than it\'s worth unless you specifically design the web content to handle `env(safe-area-inset-top)`.\n\nActually, looking at this more carefully:\n\nThe web app uses `min-h-screen` and has a header/navbar at the top. With edge-to-edge mode ON, the web content starts from y=0 (behind the status bar). The status bar overlaps the header, making buttons unclickable.\n\nThe web app does use `min-h-screen` with a fixed header. For it to work correctly, the content needs to start at the status bar height.\n\n**Best fix**: Apply window insets to the WebView\'s parent container (the FrameLayout) or to the WebView itself. Use `ViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener` to add padding equal to the system bar insets.\n\n```kotlin\nViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener(findViewById(R.id.root_container)) { view, insets ->\n    val bars = insets.getInsets(WindowInsetsCompat.Type.systemBars())\n    view.setPadding(bars.left, bars.top, bars.right, bars.bottom)\n    insets\n}\n```\n\nBut this would add padding to the FrameLayout, which would:\n1. Push the WebView content down (correct!)\n2. Also push the splashOverlay down (might look odd)\n\nActually for the splashOverlay, it should still cover the full screen including status bar area. So the overlay should NOT have the padding.\n\nBetter approach: Keep the FrameLayout full screen, add a specific container for the WebView with inset padding, keep the splashOverlay at full screen.\n\nOR: \n\n**Simplest correct approach**: Just disable edge-to-edge mode completely. This means the Android system draws the status bar normally and the WebView starts below it. The status bar color matches the app\'s dark background (`#0d1117`).\n\n```kotlin\n// Don\'t call WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)\n// This keeps the default behavior: content fits within system bars\nwindow.statusBarColor = Color.parseColor("#161b22")  // GitHub dark header color\nwindow.navigationBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")  // App background\n```\n\nThis is the most reliable fix and removes all the complexity.\n\nLet me go with the approach of:\n1. Remove `WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)` \n2. Set status bar color to match the app\'s navigation/header color (`#161b22` - GitHub dark color, or just `#0d1117`)\n3. Keep the navigation bar color matching the app background\n\nThis is the simplest and most reliable fix. It doesn\'t require any web code changes.\n\nActually, thinking about it more, for a proper Android app experience, I should handle window insets properly. Let me use the insets approach but apply it correctly:\n\nIn activity_main.xml, I\'ll add a root FrameLayout (for full-screen splash) with a child FrameLayout (for WebView with insets).\n\nActually, the cleanest approach:\n\n1. Keep `WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)` for transparent status bar\n2. But apply the window insets as padding ONLY to the WebView (not the splashOverlay)\n3. The splashOverlay still covers everything including status bar\n\n```kotlin\n// Apply insets to WebView to push content below status bar\nViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener(webView) { view, insets ->\n    val bars = insets.getInsets(WindowInsetsCompat.Type.systemBars())\n    view.setPadding(bars.left, bars.top, bars.right, bars.bottom)\n    insets\n}\n```\n\nWait but the WebView has `background = "#0d1117"`. If I add padding, the padding area would show the WebView\'s background color. That\'s fine since the background matches the app\'s dark theme.\n\nActually, the padding on the WebView itself might cause issues because the WebView renders its web content inside its padded area, but the web content itself might add its own padding thinking there\'s no system bars... this could lead to double padding.\n\nHmm, let me think differently.\n\n**The real cleanest fix for WebView + edge-to-edge**:\n\nOption A: Inject the status bar height into the web page as a CSS custom property, and add `padding-top: var(--android-status-bar-height)` to the web app\'s root element.\n\nOption B: Simply DON\'T use edge-to-edge. This is the most practical solution for a cross-platform WebView app.\n\nOption C: Use `WindowInsets` to set the WebView\'s top padding, which pushes the web content down by exactly the status bar height.\n\nFor Option C, I need to be careful: WebView\'s `setPadding` doesn\'t create a "dead zone" - it actually shifts the web content. The padding area shows the WebView\'s background color. So:\n- Status bar area: shows `#0d1117` (WebView background) - matches status bar\n- Web content: starts below status bar - correct!\n\nThis is actually correct! Let me implement Option C.\n\nBut there\'s a subtle issue: when the WebView is padded, the web CSS `height: 100vh` or `min-h-screen` might not account for the padding, potentially causing the web content to overflow.\n\nActually in WebView, `100vh` refers to the WebView\'s visible viewport, which already excludes the padding. So this should work correctly.\n\nLet me implement this:\n\n```kotlin\n// In MainActivity, after setContentView:\nViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener(webView) { view, windowInsets ->\n    val insets = windowInsets.getInsets(WindowInsetsCompat.Type.systemBars())\n    view.setPadding(0, insets.top, 0, insets.bottom)\n    windowInsets\n}\n```\n\nThis adds top padding = status bar height, bottom padding = navigation bar height.\n\nBut wait - what about the splashOverlay? It should cover the FULL screen including status bar. So the splashOverlay should NOT have the insets padding. The current layout has both WebView and splashOverlay in a FrameLayout. If I only apply padding to the WebView (not the FrameLayout), the splashOverlay will still cover full screen. \n\nThis is exactly what I want:\n- splashOverlay: full screen (covers status bar area too)\n- WebView: padded to start below status bar\n\nLet me implement this approach. This causes the top of the web content to be hidden behind/overlapping the status bar.\n\nThe fix: Use `ViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener` to apply system bar insets as padding on the WebView. This way:\n- The WebView content starts below the status bar (correct!)\n- The splashOverlay still covers full screen including status bar (still looks good)\n- The bottom of content is above the navigation bar\n\nI need to:\n1. It doesn't need padding - it should cover the entire screen. Only the WebView needs the padding.\n\nLet me write the fix:\n\n```kotlin\nimport androidx.core.view.ViewCompat\nimport androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsCompat\n\n// After splashOverlay = findViewById(...)\nViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener(webView) { view, windowInsets ->\n    val bars = windowInsets.getInsets(WindowInsetsCompat.Type.systemBars())\n    // 为 WebView 设置系统栏安全内边距，防止内容被状态栏遮挡\n    view.setPadding(bars.left, bars.top, bars.right, bars.bottom)\n    windowInsets\n}\n```\n\nThis is the targeted fix. Thought: 用户反馈正确——透明状态栏 + 边到边模式在 WebView 场景下本质上行不通：Web 内容无法像原生 View 那样精确响应 insets，导致覆盖问题持续存在。**最根本的修复**是彻底放弃边到边模式，改用与 App 背景色一致的纯色状态栏，让 Android 系统自动将内容布局到状态栏下方。
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
package com.github.manager

import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.os.Handler
import android.os.Looper
import android.view.View
import android.webkit.JavascriptInterface
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity
import androidx.core.view.ViewCompat
import androidx.core.view.WindowCompat
import androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsCompat
import androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsControllerCompat

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView
    private lateinit var splashOverlay: View

    // 防止 notifyReady 被重复调用时多次触发动画
    private var splashDismissed = false

    /**
     * JavaScript 桥接口：React 首屏渲染完成后调用 notifyReady()，
     * 通知 Android 隐藏启动遮罩。
     */
    inner class WebAppBridge {
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyReady() {
            runOnUiThread { dismissSplash() }
        }
    }

    /** 淡出并移除启动遮罩，保证只执行一次。 */
    private fun dismissSplash() {
        if (splashDismissed) return
        splashDismissed = true
        splashOverlay
            .animate()
            .alpha(0f)
            .setDuration(250)
            .withEndAction { splashOverlay.visibility = View.GONE }
            .start()
    }

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        // 全屏沉浸式：延伸到状态栏 / 导航栏下方
        WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)
        window.statusBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        WindowInsetsControllerCompat(window, window.decorView).apply {
            isAppearanceLightStatusBars = false
            isAppearanceLightNavigationBars = false
        }

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)
        splashOverlay = findViewById(R.id.splashOverlay)

        // ── 系统栏安全内边距 ──────────────────────────────────────
        // setDecorFitsSystemWindows(false) 使内容延伸到状态栏下方。
        // 在此为 WebView 单独设置 insets padding，将 Web 内容推入安全区域，
        // 避免顶部功能按钮被状态栏遮挡。splashOverlay 不受影响，仍全屏覆盖。
        ViewCompat.setOnApplyWindowInsetsListener(webView) { view, windowInsets ->
            val bars = windowInsets.getInsets(WindowInsetsCompat.Type.systemBars())
            view.setPadding(bars.left, bars.top, bars.right, bars.bottom)
            windowInsets
        }

        // ── WebView 设置 ──────────────────────────────────────────
        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true           // localStorage / sessionStorage（token 存储）
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true             // 允许读取 assets 内的文件
            allowContentAccess = true
            // 允许 file:// 脚本访问同目录其他 file:// 资源（兼容旧版 WebView）
            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
            // 允许 file:// 页面向 https:// 发起网络请求（GitHub API / OAuth）
            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }

        // WebView 背景与启动遮罩同色，避免遮罩淡出时出现颜色差异
        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor("#0d1117"))

        // ── JavaScript 桥接口 ─────────────────────────────────────
        // React 侧通过 window.AndroidBridge.notifyReady() 触发遮罩消失
        webView.addJavascriptInterface(WebAppBridge(), "AndroidBridge")

        // ── WebViewClient ─────────────────────────────────────────
        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                if (url.startsWith("file://") ||
                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
                    url.startsWith("http://")
                ) return false
                return true
            }
        }

        // ── 超时兜底：5 秒后强制消除遮罩 ────────────────────────────
        // 防止 notifyReady 因异常未被调用时遮罩永远停留
        Handler(Looper.getMainLooper()).postDelayed({ dismissSplash() }, 5000)

        // ── 加载页面 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
            webView.goBack()
        } else {
            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }
}

New String: ```
package com.github.manager

import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.os.Handler
import android.os.Looper
import android.view.View
import android.webkit.JavascriptInterface
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView
    private lateinit var splashOverlay: View

    // 防止 notifyReady 被重复调用时多次触发动画
    private var splashDismissed = false

    /**
     * JavaScript 桥接口：React 首屏渲染完成后调用 notifyReady()，
     * 通知 Android 隐藏启动遮罩。
     */
    inner class WebAppBridge {
        @JavascriptInterface
        fun notifyReady() {
            runOnUiThread { dismissSplash() }
        }
    }

    /** 淡出并移除启动遮罩，保证只执行一次。 */
    private fun dismissSplash() {
        if (splashDismissed) return
        splashDismissed = true
        splashOverlay
            .animate()
            .alpha(0f)
            .setDuration(250)
            .withEndAction { splashOverlay.visibility = View.GONE }
            .start()
    }

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        // 状态栏与导航栏使用与 App 背景相同的纯色，不使用透明 + 边到边模式。
        // 透明状态栏会导致 WebView 内容从 y=0 开始渲染，被状态栏覆盖且触摸偏移，
        // 纯色方案让 Android 系统自动将内容布局到状态栏下方，无需任何 insets 处理。
        window.statusBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)
        splashOverlay = findViewById(R.id.splashOverlay)

        // ── WebView 设置 ──────────────────────────────────────────
        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true           // localStorage / sessionStorage（token 存储）
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true             // 允许读取 assets 内的文件
            allowContentAccess = true
            // 允许 file:// 脚本访问同目录其他 file:// 资源（兼容旧版 WebView）
            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
            // 允许 file:// 页面向 https:// 发起网络请求（GitHub API / OAuth）
            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }

        // WebView 背景与启动遮罩同色，避免遮罩淡出时出现颜色差异
        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor("#0d1117"))

        // ── JavaScript 桥接口 ─────────────────────────────────────
        // React 侧通过 window.AndroidBridge.notifyReady() 触发遮罩消失
        webView.addJavascriptInterface(WebAppBridge(), "AndroidBridge")

        // ── WebViewClient ─────────────────────────────────────────
        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                if (url.startsWith("file://") ||
                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
                    url.startsWith("http://")
                ) return false
                return true
            }
        }

        // ── 超时兜底：5 秒后强制消除遮罩 ────────────────────────────
        Handler(Looper.getMainLooper()).postDelayed({ dismissSplash() }, 5000)

        // ── 加载页面 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
            webView.goBack()
        } else {
            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }
}

New String: ```
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<resources>
    <!--
      不使用透明状态栏 + 边到边模式：
      WebView 内容无法像原生 View 精确响应 insets，透明模式会导致内容被状态栏覆盖。
      改为纯色状态栏（与 App 背景同色），Android 系统自动将内容放置在状态栏下方。
    -->
    <style name="Theme.GitHubManager" parent="Theme.AppCompat.Light.NoActionBar">
        <!-- 窗口背景与 App 深色背景一致，防止冷启动闪白 -->
        <item name="android:windowBackground">#0d1117</item>
        <!-- 状态栏颜色由 MainActivity 代码设置，此处设为与背景一致的默认值 -->
        <item name="android:statusBarColor">#0d1117</item>
        <item name="android:navigationBarColor">#0d1117</item>
        <!-- API 28+ 刘海屏延伸；低版本自动忽略 -->
        <item name="android:windowLayoutInDisplayCutoutMode">shortEdges</item>
    </style>
</resources>

    16	class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {
    17	
    18	    private lateinit var webView: WebView
    19	    private lateinit var splashOverlay: View
    20	
    21	    // 防止 notifyReady 被重复调用时多次触发动画
    22	    private var splashDismissed = false
    23	
    24	    /**
    25	     * JavaScript 桥接口：React 首屏渲染完成后调用 notifyReady()，
    26	     * 通知 Android 隐藏启动遮罩。
    27	     */
    28	    inner class WebAppBridge {
    29	        @JavascriptInterface
    30	        fun notifyReady() {
    31	            runOnUiThread { dismissSplash() }
    32	        }
    33	    }
    34	
    35	    /** 淡出并移除启动遮罩，保证只执行一次。 */
    36	    private fun dismissSplash() {
    37	        if (splashDismissed) return
    38	        splashDismissed = true
    39	        splashOverlay
    40	            .animate()
    41	            .alpha(0f)
    42	            .setDuration(250)
    43	            .withEndAction { splashOverlay.visibility = View.GONE }
    44	            .start()
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    48	    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
    49	        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)
    50	
    51	        // 状态栏与导航栏使用与 App 背景相同的纯色，不使用透明 + 边到边模式。
    52	        // 透明状态栏会导致 WebView 内容从 y=0 开始渲染，被状态栏覆盖且触摸偏移，
    53	        // 纯色方案让 Android 系统自动将内容布局到状态栏下方，无需任何 insets 处理。
    54	        window.statusBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")
    55	        window.navigationBarColor = Color.parseColor("#0d1117")
    56	
    57	        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)
    58	
    59	        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)
    60	        splashOverlay = findViewById(R.id.splashOverlay)
    61	
    62	        // ── WebView 设置 ──────────────────────────────────────────
    63	        webView.settings.apply {
    64	            javaScriptEnabled = true
    65	            domStorageEnabled = true           // localStorage / sessionStorage（token 存储）
    66	            databaseEnabled = true
    67	            allowFileAccess = true             // 允许读取 assets 内的文件
    68	            allowContentAccess = true
    69	            // 允许 file:// 脚本访问同目录其他 file:// 资源（兼容旧版 WebView）
    70	            @Suppress("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    71	            allowFileAccessFromFileURLs = true
    72	            // 允许 file:// 页面向 https:// 发起网络请求（GitHub API / OAuth）
    73	            allowUniversalAccessFromFileURLs = true
    74	            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
    75	            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
    76	            useWideViewPort = true
    77	            loadWithOverviewMode = true
    78	            setSupportZoom(false)
    79	            displayZoomControls = false
    80	            builtInZoomControls = false
    81	            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        // WebView 背景与启动遮罩同色，避免遮罩淡出时出现颜色差异
    85	        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.parseColor("#0d1117"))
    86	
    87	        // ── JavaScript 桥接口 ─────────────────────────────────────
    88	        // React 侧通过 window.AndroidBridge.notifyReady() 触发遮罩消失
    89	        webView.addJavascriptInterface(WebAppBridge(), "AndroidBridge")
    90	
    91	        // ── WebViewClient ─────────────────────────────────────────
    92	        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
    93	            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
    94	                view: WebView?,
    95	                request: WebResourceRequest?,
    96	            ): Boolean {
    97	                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
    98	                if (url.startsWith("file://") ||
    99	                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
   100	                    url.startsWith("http://")
   101	                ) return false
   102	                return true
   103	            }
   104	        }
   105	
   106	        // ── 超时兜底：5 秒后强制消除遮罩 ────────────────────────────
   107	        Handler(Looper.getMainLooper()).postDelayed({ dismissSplash() }, 5000)
   108	
   109	        // ── 加载页面 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
   110	        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
   111	            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
   112	        } else {
   113	            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
   114	        }
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
   118	        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
   119	        webView.saveState(outState)
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
   123	    override fun onBackPressed() {
   124	        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
   125	            webView.goBack()
   126	        } else {
   127	            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
   128	            super.onBackPressed()
   129	        }
   130	    }

            DownloadManager.Request.VISIBILITY_VISIBLE_NOTIFY_COMPLETED\n                    )\n                    setDestinationInExternalPublicDir(Environment.DIRECTORY_DOWNLOADS, fileName)\n getSystemService(DOWNLOAD_SERVICE) as DownloadManager\n                dm.enqueue(request)\n                Toast.makeText(this, "开始下载：$fileName", Toast.LENGTH_SHORT).show()\n            } catch (e:
